1. Platform Overview &amp; Architecture
<w:left w:val="single" w:color="auto" w:sz="4"/><w:bottom w:val="single" w:color="auto" w:sz="4"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="auto" w:sz="4"/><w:insideH w:val="single" w:color="auto" w:sz="4"/><w:insideV w:val="single" w:color="auto" w:sz="4"/></w:tblBorders></w:tblPr><w:gridCol w:w="9360"/></w:tblGrid><w:left w:val="single" w:color="CCCCCC" w:sz="1"/><w:bottom w:val="single" w:color="CCCCCC" w:sz="1"/><w:right w:val="single" w:color="CCCCCC" w:sz="1"/></w:tcBorders><w:shd w:fill="D6E8F7" w:val="clear"/><w:left w:type="dxa" w:w="200"/><w:bottom w:type="dxa" w:w="120"/><w:right w:type="dxa" w:w="200"/></w:tcMar></w:tcPr><w:p><w:pPr><w:spacing w:after="80"/></w:pPr><w:r><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="Arial" w:cs="Arial" w:eastAsia="Arial" w:hAnsi="Arial"/><w:b/><w:bCs/><w:color w:val="1A3C6E"/><w:sz w:val="22"/><w:szCs w:val="22"/></w:rPr>What is This Platform?
A full-featured online and home tutoring marketplace that connects students and parents with verified tutors across Pakistan and internationally. It handles the complete lifecycle: discovery â†’ booking â†’ session delivery â†’ payment â†’ review.

1.1 Platform Type
This is a two-sided marketplace platform with three user types: Students/Parents, Tutors, and Admins. Each user type has a dedicated workflow, dashboard, and set of permissions.
